msg:The hotel is about 500 meters away from the ski resort. I hesitated between Holiday Inn and Crown Hotel because of this, but later I found it unnecessary. The shuttle bus is available at any time, which is very convenient. It takes only three minutes to get to the gate. The hotel has a ski equipment hall, so you don't need to queue up. There will be a car waiting for you at the door after changing your equipment. The service staff is responsive and the breakfast is okay. The room is not as luxurious as Prince Hotel, but it is new. The disadvantage is that the heating is overheated in the first few days. It is so hot that I have to keep the window open and sweat profusely, and there is no way to turn it down. I didn't sleep well for two days, and then the temperature was lowered. Tonghua Ski Resort has few people, good snow and cheap prices. Overall, it is very cost-effective.
